int hConn, hReq, rc, len; CComBSTR strQuery, colDef, table_name, column_name; T_CCI_ERROR error; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID || !pColumnDesc) || (pColumnDesc->cPropertySets > 0 && !pColumnDesc->rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다. table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); len = table_name.Length(); if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"') { table_name.Empty(); table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1); table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0'; } //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } { //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); //컬럼 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc >= 0) //modified 2003.07.09 return DB_E_DUPLICATECOLUMNID; cci_close_req_handle(hReq); } strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" ADD ATTRIBUTE "); if (IsValidDBID(&pColumnDesc->dbcid) != S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (CompareDBIDs(&pColumnDesc->dbcid, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (pColumnDesc->dbcid.eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (!pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; column_name.Append(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName); //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; strQuery.Append(column_name); strQuery.Append(L" "); hr = Type::GetColumnDefinitionString(*pColumnDesc, colDef); if (FAILED(hr)) return hr; strQuery.Append(colDef); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); //ppColumnID에 생성된컬럼 이름을 넘겨준다. if(ppColumnID) { *ppColumnID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); DBID colID; colID.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; colID.uName.pwszName = column_name; CopyDBIDs(*ppColumnID, &colID); } return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pColumnID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; int hConn, hReq, rc, len; CComBSTR strQuery = NULL, table_name; T_CCI_ERROR error; CDBIDOps op; ClearError(); if (!pTableID || !pColumnID) return E_INVALIDARG; if (op.IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.IsValidDBID(pColumnID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pColumnID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (pColumnID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (!pColumnID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다. table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); len = table_name.Length(); if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"') { table_name.Empty(); table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1); table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0'; } //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Table이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //Column이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnID->uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return E_FAIL; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" DROP "); strQuery.Append(pColumnID->uName.pwszName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::CreateIndex( /* [in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [in] */ DBID *pIndexID, /* [in] */ DBORDINAL cIndexColumnDescs, /* [size_is][in] */ const DBINDEXCOLUMNDESC rgIndexColumnDescs[], /* [in] */ ULONG cPropertySets, /* [size_is][out][in] */ DBPROPSET rgPropertySets[], /* [out] */ DBID **ppIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; bool bIsUnique = false; if (ppIndexID) *ppIndexID = NULL; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID) || (!pIndexID && !ppIndexID) || (!cIndexColumnDescs) || (!rgIndexColumnDescs) || (cPropertySets && !rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (pIndexID) { if (CompareDBIDs(pIndexID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; if ((pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_GUID_NAME || pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_NAME) && (!pIndexID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pIndexID->uName.pwszName))) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; } //프로퍼티 검사 for (ULONG k = 0; k < cPropertySets; k++) { DBPROPSET propSet = rgPropertySets[k]; if (propSet.cProperties && !propSet.rgProperties) return E_INVALIDARG; if (propSet.guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_INDEX) { for (ULONG i = 0; i < propSet.cProperties; i++) { DBPROPID property = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwPropertyID; DBPROPSTATUS* status = &propSet.rgProperties[i].dwStatus; DBPROPOPTIONS options = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwOptions; VARIANT val = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue; VARTYPE type = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue.vt; if (CompareDBIDs(&propSet.rgProperties[i].colid, &DB_NULLID) != S_OK) hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; if (property == DBPROP_INDEX_AUTOUPDATE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_PRIMARYKEY || property == DBPROP_INDEX_CLUSTERED || property == DBPROP_INDEX_SORTBOOKMARKS || property == DBPROP_INDEX_FILLFACTOR || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TEMPINDEX || property == DBPROP_INDEX_INITIALSIZE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TYPE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLCOLLATION || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLS) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_NOTSUPPORTED; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else { if (options != DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED && options != DBPROPOPTIONS_OPTIONAL) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADOPTION; return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } *status = DBPROPSTATUS_OK; if (type != VT_BOOL) //Type Error { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADVALUE; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) { return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; } bIsUnique = (V_BOOL(&val)==VARIANT_TRUE); } } } } hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (!pIndexID) { indexName.Append(L"i_"); indexName.Append(tableName); indexName.Append(L"_"); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { indexName.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i+1 != cIndexColumnDescs) indexName.Append(L"_"); } } else indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //인덱스 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(ITableDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) return DB_E_DUPLICATEINDEXID; rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (bIsUnique) strQuery.Append(L"CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"CREATE INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); strQuery.Append(L" ("); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { //컬럼 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), CW2A(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i + 1 != cIndexColumnDescs) strQuery.Append(L","); } strQuery.Append(L")"); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } if(ppIndexID) { DBID tmp; tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; tmp.uName.pwszName = indexName; *ppIndexID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); CopyDBIDs(*ppIndexID, &tmp); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropIndex( /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pTableID) return E_INVALIDARG; ClearError(); hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (pIndexID) { bool indexFound = false; bool bIsUniqueIndex = false; indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //Index 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOINDEX; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int isUnique; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 1, CCI_A_TYPE_INT, &isUnique, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) { indexFound = true; if (isUnique == 0) bIsUniqueIndex = true; break; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (!indexFound) return DB_E_NOINDEX; if (bIsUniqueIndex) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } else { CAtlArray<CStringA> rgIndexNames; CAtlArray<int> rgIndexTypes; hr = Util::GetIndexNamesInTable(hConn, CW2A(tableName), rgIndexNames, rgIndexTypes); if (FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; size_t cIndex = rgIndexNames.GetCount(); for(size_t i=0;i<cIndex;i++) { if (rgIndexTypes.GetAt(i) == 0) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(rgIndexNames[i].GetBuffer()); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); if (i+1 != cIndex) strQuery.Append(L";"); } hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } AutoCommit(0); return hr; }
594  strQuery.Append(L")");
595 
596  char flag = 0;
597 
598  if (Util::RequestedRIIDNeedsUpdatability(riid))
599  flag |= (CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID | CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE);
600  for (ULONG i = 0; i < cPropertySets; i++)
601  {
602  if (rgPropertySets[i].guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_ROWSET)
603  {
604  ULONG cProp = rgPropertySets[i].cProperties;
605  for (ULONG j = 0; j < cProp; j++)
606  {
607  DBPROPID propID = rgPropertySets[i].rgProperties[j].dwPropertyID;
608  if (propID == DBPROP_IRowsetChange ||
609  propID == DBPROP_IRowsetUpdate ||
610  propID == DBPROP_IRow ||
611  propID == DBPROP_IGetRow ||
612  propID == DBPROP_IGetSession ||
613  propID == DBPROP_OTHERUPDATEDELETE)
614  {
615  flag |= (CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID | CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE);
616  break;
617  }
618  }
619 
620  }
621  }
622 
623  hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), flag, &error);
624  if (hReq < 0)
625  {
626  ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg);
627  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
628  }
629  rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error);
630  if (rc < 0)
631  {
632  ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg);
633  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
634  }
635  AutoCommit(0);
636 
637  DBID tmp;
638  tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME;
639  tmp.uName.pwszName = tableName;
640 
641  //ppRowset이 NULL이 아닌 경우 Rowset을 연다.
642  if (ppRowset)
643  {
644  HRESULT _hr = OpenRowset(pUnkOuter, &tmp, NULL, riid, cPropertySets, rgPropertySets, ppRowset);
645  if (FAILED(_hr))
646  {
647  return _hr;
648  }
649 
650  //위에서 DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED등이 발생하지 않았었으면 hr을 다시 세팅한다.
651  if (hr == S_OK) hr = _hr;
652  }
653 
654  //ppTableID에 생성된 테이블 이름을 넘겨준다.
655  if(ppTableID)
656  {
657  *ppTableID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID));
658  CopyDBIDs(*ppTableID, &tmp);
659  }
660 
661  return hr;
662 }

664 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropTable(DBID *pTableID)
665 {
666  HRESULT hr = S_OK;
667  int hConn, hReq, rc, len;
668  CComBSTR strQuery = NULL;
669  CComBSTR table_name;
670  T_CCI_ERROR error;
671  CDBIDOps op;
672 
673  ClearError();
674 
675  if (!pTableID)
676  return E_INVALIDARG;
677 
678  if (op.IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK)
679  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
680  if (op.CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK)
681  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
682  if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME)
683  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
684  if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName))
685  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
686 
687  //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다.
688  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName);
689  len = table_name.Length();
690  if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"')
691  {
692  table_name.Empty();
693  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1);
694  table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0';
695  }
696 
697  //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크
698  if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen)
699  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
700 
701  //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크
702  if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars))
703  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
704 
705  hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn);
706 
707  //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hr = Util::DoesTableExist(hConn, CW2A(table_name)); if(FAILED(hr)) return hr; if(hr==S_FALSE) return DB_E_NOTABLE; strQuery.Append(L"DROP TABLE "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::AddColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBCOLUMNDESC *pColumnDesc, DBID **ppColumnID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; int hConn, hReq, rc, len; CComBSTR strQuery, colDef, table_name, column_name; T_CCI_ERROR error; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID || !pColumnDesc) || (pColumnDesc->cPropertySets > 0 && !pColumnDesc->rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다. table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); len = table_name.Length(); if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"') { table_name.Empty(); table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1); table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0'; } //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } { //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); //컬럼 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc >= 0) //modified 2003.07.09 return DB_E_DUPLICATECOLUMNID; cci_close_req_handle(hReq); } strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" ADD ATTRIBUTE "); if (IsValidDBID(&pColumnDesc->dbcid) != S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (CompareDBIDs(&pColumnDesc->dbcid, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (pColumnDesc->dbcid.eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (!pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; column_name.Append(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName); //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; strQuery.Append(column_name); strQuery.Append(L" "); hr = Type::GetColumnDefinitionString(*pColumnDesc, colDef); if (FAILED(hr)) return hr; strQuery.Append(colDef); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); //ppColumnID에 생성된컬럼 이름을 넘겨준다. if(ppColumnID) { *ppColumnID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); DBID colID; colID.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; colID.uName.pwszName = column_name; CopyDBIDs(*ppColumnID, &colID); } return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pColumnID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; int hConn, hReq, rc, len; CComBSTR strQuery = NULL, table_name; T_CCI_ERROR error; CDBIDOps op; ClearError(); if (!pTableID || !pColumnID) return E_INVALIDARG; if (op.IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.IsValidDBID(pColumnID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pColumnID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (pColumnID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (!pColumnID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다. table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); len = table_name.Length(); if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"') { table_name.Empty(); table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1); table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0'; } //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Table이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //Column이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnID->uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return E_FAIL; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" DROP "); strQuery.Append(pColumnID->uName.pwszName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::CreateIndex( /* [in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [in] */ DBID *pIndexID, /* [in] */ DBORDINAL cIndexColumnDescs, /* [size_is][in] */ const DBINDEXCOLUMNDESC rgIndexColumnDescs[], /* [in] */ ULONG cPropertySets, /* [size_is][out][in] */ DBPROPSET rgPropertySets[], /* [out] */ DBID **ppIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; bool bIsUnique = false; if (ppIndexID) *ppIndexID = NULL; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID) || (!pIndexID && !ppIndexID) || (!cIndexColumnDescs) || (!rgIndexColumnDescs) || (cPropertySets && !rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (pIndexID) { if (CompareDBIDs(pIndexID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; if ((pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_GUID_NAME || pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_NAME) && (!pIndexID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pIndexID->uName.pwszName))) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; } //프로퍼티 검사 for (ULONG k = 0; k < cPropertySets; k++) { DBPROPSET propSet = rgPropertySets[k]; if (propSet.cProperties && !propSet.rgProperties) return E_INVALIDARG; if (propSet.guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_INDEX) { for (ULONG i = 0; i < propSet.cProperties; i++) { DBPROPID property = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwPropertyID; DBPROPSTATUS* status = &propSet.rgProperties[i].dwStatus; DBPROPOPTIONS options = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwOptions; VARIANT val = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue; VARTYPE type = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue.vt; if (CompareDBIDs(&propSet.rgProperties[i].colid, &DB_NULLID) != S_OK) hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; if (property == DBPROP_INDEX_AUTOUPDATE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_PRIMARYKEY || property == DBPROP_INDEX_CLUSTERED || property == DBPROP_INDEX_SORTBOOKMARKS || property == DBPROP_INDEX_FILLFACTOR || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TEMPINDEX || property == DBPROP_INDEX_INITIALSIZE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TYPE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLCOLLATION || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLS) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_NOTSUPPORTED; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else { if (options != DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED && options != DBPROPOPTIONS_OPTIONAL) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADOPTION; return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } *status = DBPROPSTATUS_OK; if (type != VT_BOOL) //Type Error { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADVALUE; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) { return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; } bIsUnique = (V_BOOL(&val)==VARIANT_TRUE); } } } } hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (!pIndexID) { indexName.Append(L"i_"); indexName.Append(tableName); indexName.Append(L"_"); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { indexName.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i+1 != cIndexColumnDescs) indexName.Append(L"_"); } } else indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //인덱스 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(ITableDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) return DB_E_DUPLICATEINDEXID; rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (bIsUnique) strQuery.Append(L"CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"CREATE INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); strQuery.Append(L" ("); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { //컬럼 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), CW2A(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i + 1 != cIndexColumnDescs) strQuery.Append(L","); } strQuery.Append(L")"); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } if(ppIndexID) { DBID tmp; tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; tmp.uName.pwszName = indexName; *ppIndexID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); CopyDBIDs(*ppIndexID, &tmp); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropIndex( /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pTableID) return E_INVALIDARG; ClearError(); hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (pIndexID) { bool indexFound = false; bool bIsUniqueIndex = false; indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //Index 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOINDEX; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int isUnique; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 1, CCI_A_TYPE_INT, &isUnique, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) { indexFound = true; if (isUnique == 0) bIsUniqueIndex = true; break; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (!indexFound) return DB_E_NOINDEX; if (bIsUniqueIndex) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } else { CAtlArray<CStringA> rgIndexNames; CAtlArray<int> rgIndexTypes; hr = Util::GetIndexNamesInTable(hConn, CW2A(tableName), rgIndexNames, rgIndexTypes); if (FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; size_t cIndex = rgIndexNames.GetCount(); for(size_t i=0;i<cIndex;i++) { if (rgIndexTypes.GetAt(i) == 0) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(rgIndexNames[i].GetBuffer()); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); if (i+1 != cIndex) strQuery.Append(L";"); } hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } AutoCommit(0); return hr; }
708  hr = Util::DoesTableExist(hConn, CW2A(table_name));
709  if(FAILED(hr))
710  return hr;

712  return DB_E_NOTABLE;

732 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::AddColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBCOLUMNDESC *pColumnDesc, DBID **ppColumnID)
733 {
734  HRESULT hr = S_OK;
735  int hConn, hReq, rc, len;
736  CComBSTR strQuery, colDef, table_name, column_name;
737  T_CCI_ERROR error;
738 
739  ClearError();
740 
741  if ((!pTableID || !pColumnDesc) ||
742  (pColumnDesc->cPropertySets > 0 && !pColumnDesc->rgPropertySets))
743  return E_INVALIDARG;
744 
745  if (IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK)
746  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
747  if (CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK)
748  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
749  if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME)
750  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
751  if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName))
752  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
753 
754  //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다.
755  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName);
756  len = table_name.Length();
757  if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"')
758  {
759  table_name.Empty();
760  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1);
761  table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0';
762  }
763 
764  //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크
765  if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen)
766  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
767  //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크
768  if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars))
769  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
770 
771  hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn);
772  if (FAILED(hr))
773  {
774  return E_FAIL;
775  }
776 
777  {
778  //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); //컬럼 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc >= 0) //modified 2003.07.09 return DB_E_DUPLICATECOLUMNID; cci_close_req_handle(hReq); } strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" ADD ATTRIBUTE "); if (IsValidDBID(&pColumnDesc->dbcid) != S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (CompareDBIDs(&pColumnDesc->dbcid, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (pColumnDesc->dbcid.eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; if (!pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; column_name.Append(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName); //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID; strQuery.Append(column_name); strQuery.Append(L" "); hr = Type::GetColumnDefinitionString(*pColumnDesc, colDef); if (FAILED(hr)) return hr; strQuery.Append(colDef); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); //ppColumnID에 생성된컬럼 이름을 넘겨준다. if(ppColumnID) { *ppColumnID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); DBID colID; colID.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; colID.uName.pwszName = column_name; CopyDBIDs(*ppColumnID, &colID); } return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pColumnID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; int hConn, hReq, rc, len; CComBSTR strQuery = NULL, table_name; T_CCI_ERROR error; CDBIDOps op; ClearError(); if (!pTableID || !pColumnID) return E_INVALIDARG; if (op.IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; if (op.IsValidDBID(pColumnID) != S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (op.CompareDBIDs(pColumnID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (pColumnID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; if (!pColumnID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다. table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); len = table_name.Length(); if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"') { table_name.Empty(); table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1); table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0'; } //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Table이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOTABLE; //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크 if (wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; //Column이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크 if (wcspbrk(pColumnID->uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars)) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return E_FAIL; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" DROP "); strQuery.Append(pColumnID->uName.pwszName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::CreateIndex( /* [in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [in] */ DBID *pIndexID, /* [in] */ DBORDINAL cIndexColumnDescs, /* [size_is][in] */ const DBINDEXCOLUMNDESC rgIndexColumnDescs[], /* [in] */ ULONG cPropertySets, /* [size_is][out][in] */ DBPROPSET rgPropertySets[], /* [out] */ DBID **ppIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; bool bIsUnique = false; if (ppIndexID) *ppIndexID = NULL; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID) || (!pIndexID && !ppIndexID) || (!cIndexColumnDescs) || (!rgIndexColumnDescs) || (cPropertySets && !rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (pIndexID) { if (CompareDBIDs(pIndexID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; if ((pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_GUID_NAME || pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_NAME) && (!pIndexID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pIndexID->uName.pwszName))) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; } //프로퍼티 검사 for (ULONG k = 0; k < cPropertySets; k++) { DBPROPSET propSet = rgPropertySets[k]; if (propSet.cProperties && !propSet.rgProperties) return E_INVALIDARG; if (propSet.guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_INDEX) { for (ULONG i = 0; i < propSet.cProperties; i++) { DBPROPID property = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwPropertyID; DBPROPSTATUS* status = &propSet.rgProperties[i].dwStatus; DBPROPOPTIONS options = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwOptions; VARIANT val = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue; VARTYPE type = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue.vt; if (CompareDBIDs(&propSet.rgProperties[i].colid, &DB_NULLID) != S_OK) hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; if (property == DBPROP_INDEX_AUTOUPDATE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_PRIMARYKEY || property == DBPROP_INDEX_CLUSTERED || property == DBPROP_INDEX_SORTBOOKMARKS || property == DBPROP_INDEX_FILLFACTOR || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TEMPINDEX || property == DBPROP_INDEX_INITIALSIZE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TYPE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLCOLLATION || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLS) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_NOTSUPPORTED; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else { if (options != DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED && options != DBPROPOPTIONS_OPTIONAL) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADOPTION; return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } *status = DBPROPSTATUS_OK; if (type != VT_BOOL) //Type Error { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADVALUE; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) { return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; } bIsUnique = (V_BOOL(&val)==VARIANT_TRUE); } } } } hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (!pIndexID) { indexName.Append(L"i_"); indexName.Append(tableName); indexName.Append(L"_"); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { indexName.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i+1 != cIndexColumnDescs) indexName.Append(L"_"); } } else indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //인덱스 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(ITableDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) return DB_E_DUPLICATEINDEXID; rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (bIsUnique) strQuery.Append(L"CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"CREATE INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); strQuery.Append(L" ("); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { //컬럼 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), CW2A(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i + 1 != cIndexColumnDescs) strQuery.Append(L","); } strQuery.Append(L")"); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } if(ppIndexID) { DBID tmp; tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; tmp.uName.pwszName = indexName; *ppIndexID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); CopyDBIDs(*ppIndexID, &tmp); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropIndex( /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pTableID) return E_INVALIDARG; ClearError(); hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (pIndexID) { bool indexFound = false; bool bIsUniqueIndex = false; indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //Index 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOINDEX; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int isUnique; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 1, CCI_A_TYPE_INT, &isUnique, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) { indexFound = true; if (isUnique == 0) bIsUniqueIndex = true; break; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (!indexFound) return DB_E_NOINDEX; if (bIsUniqueIndex) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } else { CAtlArray<CStringA> rgIndexNames; CAtlArray<int> rgIndexTypes; hr = Util::GetIndexNamesInTable(hConn, CW2A(tableName), rgIndexNames, rgIndexTypes); if (FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; size_t cIndex = rgIndexNames.GetCount(); for(size_t i=0;i<cIndex;i++) { if (rgIndexTypes.GetAt(i) == 0) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(rgIndexNames[i].GetBuffer()); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); if (i+1 != cIndex) strQuery.Append(L";"); } hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } AutoCommit(0); return hr; }

} rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::CreateIndex( /* [in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [in] */ DBID *pIndexID, /* [in] */ DBORDINAL cIndexColumnDescs, /* [size_is][in] */ const DBINDEXCOLUMNDESC rgIndexColumnDescs[], /* [in] */ ULONG cPropertySets, /* [size_is][out][in] */ DBPROPSET rgPropertySets[], /* [out] */ DBID **ppIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; bool bIsUnique = false; if (ppIndexID) *ppIndexID = NULL; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID) || (!pIndexID && !ppIndexID) || (!cIndexColumnDescs) || (!rgIndexColumnDescs) || (cPropertySets && !rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (pIndexID) { if (CompareDBIDs(pIndexID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; if ((pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_GUID_NAME || pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_NAME) && (!pIndexID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pIndexID->uName.pwszName))) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; } //프로퍼티 검사 for (ULONG k = 0; k < cPropertySets; k++) { DBPROPSET propSet = rgPropertySets[k]; if (propSet.cProperties && !propSet.rgProperties) return E_INVALIDARG; if (propSet.guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_INDEX) { for (ULONG i = 0; i < propSet.cProperties; i++) { DBPROPID property = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwPropertyID; DBPROPSTATUS* status = &propSet.rgProperties[i].dwStatus; DBPROPOPTIONS options = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwOptions; VARIANT val = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue; VARTYPE type = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue.vt; if (CompareDBIDs(&propSet.rgProperties[i].colid, &DB_NULLID) != S_OK) hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; if (property == DBPROP_INDEX_AUTOUPDATE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_PRIMARYKEY || property == DBPROP_INDEX_CLUSTERED || property == DBPROP_INDEX_SORTBOOKMARKS || property == DBPROP_INDEX_FILLFACTOR || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TEMPINDEX || property == DBPROP_INDEX_INITIALSIZE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TYPE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLCOLLATION || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLS) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_NOTSUPPORTED; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else { if (options != DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED && options != DBPROPOPTIONS_OPTIONAL) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADOPTION; return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } *status = DBPROPSTATUS_OK; if (type != VT_BOOL) //Type Error { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADVALUE; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) { return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; } bIsUnique = (V_BOOL(&val)==VARIANT_TRUE); } } } } hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (!pIndexID) { indexName.Append(L"i_"); indexName.Append(tableName); indexName.Append(L"_"); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { indexName.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i+1 != cIndexColumnDescs) indexName.Append(L"_"); } } else indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //인덱스 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(ITableDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) return DB_E_DUPLICATEINDEXID; rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (bIsUnique) strQuery.Append(L"CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"CREATE INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); strQuery.Append(L" ("); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { //컬럼 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), CW2A(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i + 1 != cIndexColumnDescs) strQuery.Append(L","); } strQuery.Append(L")"); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } if(ppIndexID) { DBID tmp; tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; tmp.uName.pwszName = indexName; *ppIndexID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); CopyDBIDs(*ppIndexID, &tmp); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropIndex( /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pTableID) return E_INVALIDARG; ClearError(); hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (pIndexID) { bool indexFound = false; bool bIsUniqueIndex = false; indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //Index 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOINDEX; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int isUnique; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 1, CCI_A_TYPE_INT, &isUnique, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) { indexFound = true; if (isUnique == 0) bIsUniqueIndex = true; break; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (!indexFound) return DB_E_NOINDEX; if (bIsUniqueIndex) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } else { CAtlArray<CStringA> rgIndexNames; CAtlArray<int> rgIndexTypes; hr = Util::GetIndexNamesInTable(hConn, CW2A(tableName), rgIndexNames, rgIndexTypes); if (FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; size_t cIndex = rgIndexNames.GetCount(); for(size_t i=0;i<cIndex;i++) { if (rgIndexTypes.GetAt(i) == 0) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(rgIndexNames[i].GetBuffer()); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); if (i+1 != cIndex) strQuery.Append(L";"); } hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } AutoCommit(0); return hr; }
793  hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name),
794  CW2A(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName), 0, &error);
795  if(hReq<0)
796  {
797  ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n");
798  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
799  }
800  rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error);
801  if(rc >= 0) //modified 2003.07.09
802  return DB_E_DUPLICATECOLUMNID;
803 
804  cci_close_req_handle(hReq);
805  }
806 
807  strQuery.Append(L"ALTER ");
808  strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName);
809  strQuery.Append(L" ADD ATTRIBUTE ");
810 
811  if (IsValidDBID(&pColumnDesc->dbcid) != S_OK)
812  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
813  if (CompareDBIDs(&pColumnDesc->dbcid, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK)
814  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
815  if (pColumnDesc->dbcid.eKind != DBKIND_NAME)
816  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
817  if (!pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName))
818  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
819 
820  column_name.Append(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName);
821 
822  //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크
823  if (wcslen(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen)
824  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
825  //Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크
826  if (wcspbrk(pColumnDesc->dbcid.uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars))
827  return DB_E_BADCOLUMNID;
828 
829  strQuery.Append(column_name);
830  strQuery.Append(L" ");
831  hr = Type::GetColumnDefinitionString(*pColumnDesc, colDef);
832  if (FAILED(hr))
833  return hr;
834  strQuery.Append(colDef);
835 
836  hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error);
837  if (hReq < 0)
838  {
839  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
840  }
841 
842  rc = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &error);
843  if (rc < 0)
844  {
845  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
846  }
847 
848  AutoCommit(0);
849 
850  //ppColumnID에 생성된컬럼 이름을 넘겨준다.
851  if(ppColumnID)
852  {
853  *ppColumnID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID));
854  DBID colID;
855  colID.eKind = DBKIND_NAME;
856  colID.uName.pwszName = column_name;
857  CopyDBIDs(*ppColumnID, &colID);
858  }
859 
860  return hr;
861 }

863 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropColumn(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pColumnID)
864 {
865  HRESULT hr = S_OK;
866  int hConn, hReq, rc, len;
867  CComBSTR strQuery = NULL, table_name;
868  T_CCI_ERROR error;
869  CDBIDOps op;
870 
871  ClearError();
872 
873  if (!pTableID || !pColumnID)
874  return E_INVALIDARG;
875 
876  if (op.IsValidDBID(pTableID) != S_OK)
877  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
878  if (op.CompareDBIDs(pTableID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK)
879  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
880  if (pTableID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME)
881  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
882  if (!pTableID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName))
883  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
884 
885  if (op.IsValidDBID(pColumnID) != S_OK)
886  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
887  if (op.CompareDBIDs(pColumnID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK)
888  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
889  if (pColumnID->eKind != DBKIND_NAME)
890  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
891  if (!pColumnID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName))
892  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
893 
894  //quoted table name인 경우 quotation을 삭제한다.
895  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName);
896  len = table_name.Length();
897  if (table_name.m_str[0] == '\"' && table_name.m_str[len - 1] == '\"')
898  {
899  table_name.Empty();
900  table_name.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName + 1);
901  table_name.m_str[len - 2] = '\0';
902  }
903 
904  //Maximum Table Length를 넘는지 체크
905  if (wcslen(table_name) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].cchMaxLen)
906  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
907  //Table이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크
908  if (wcspbrk(table_name, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[8].pwszInvalidChars))
909  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
910 
911  //Maximum Column Length를 넘는지 체크
912  if (wcslen(pColumnID->uName.pwszName) > ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].cchMaxLen)
913  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
914  //Column이 Invalid character를 포함하는지 체크
915  if (wcspbrk(pColumnID->uName.pwszName, ProvInfo::LiteralInfos[2].pwszInvalidChars))
916  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
917 
918  hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn);
919  if (FAILED(hr))
920  {
921  return E_FAIL;
922  }
923 
924  //테이블 이름이 있는지 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name), CW2A(pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return E_FAIL; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(L"ALTER "); strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName); strQuery.Append(L" DROP "); strQuery.Append(pColumnID->uName.pwszName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::CreateIndex( /* [in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [in] */ DBID *pIndexID, /* [in] */ DBORDINAL cIndexColumnDescs, /* [size_is][in] */ const DBINDEXCOLUMNDESC rgIndexColumnDescs[], /* [in] */ ULONG cPropertySets, /* [size_is][out][in] */ DBPROPSET rgPropertySets[], /* [out] */ DBID **ppIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; bool bIsUnique = false; if (ppIndexID) *ppIndexID = NULL; ClearError(); if ((!pTableID) || (!pIndexID && !ppIndexID) || (!cIndexColumnDescs) || (!rgIndexColumnDescs) || (cPropertySets && !rgPropertySets)) return E_INVALIDARG; if (pIndexID) { if (CompareDBIDs(pIndexID, &DB_NULLID) == S_OK) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; if ((pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_GUID_NAME || pIndexID->eKind == DBKIND_NAME) && (!pIndexID->uName.pwszName || !wcslen(pIndexID->uName.pwszName))) return DB_E_BADINDEXID; } //프로퍼티 검사 for (ULONG k = 0; k < cPropertySets; k++) { DBPROPSET propSet = rgPropertySets[k]; if (propSet.cProperties && !propSet.rgProperties) return E_INVALIDARG; if (propSet.guidPropertySet == DBPROPSET_INDEX) { for (ULONG i = 0; i < propSet.cProperties; i++) { DBPROPID property = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwPropertyID; DBPROPSTATUS* status = &propSet.rgProperties[i].dwStatus; DBPROPOPTIONS options = propSet.rgProperties[i].dwOptions; VARIANT val = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue; VARTYPE type = propSet.rgProperties[i].vValue.vt; if (CompareDBIDs(&propSet.rgProperties[i].colid, &DB_NULLID) != S_OK) hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; if (property == DBPROP_INDEX_AUTOUPDATE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_PRIMARYKEY || property == DBPROP_INDEX_CLUSTERED || property == DBPROP_INDEX_SORTBOOKMARKS || property == DBPROP_INDEX_FILLFACTOR || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TEMPINDEX || property == DBPROP_INDEX_INITIALSIZE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_TYPE || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLCOLLATION || property == DBPROP_INDEX_NULLS) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_NOTSUPPORTED; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else { if (options != DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED && options != DBPROPOPTIONS_OPTIONAL) { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADOPTION; return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } *status = DBPROPSTATUS_OK; if (type != VT_BOOL) //Type Error { *status = DBPROPSTATUS_BADVALUE; if (options == DBPROPOPTIONS_REQUIRED) { return DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } else hr = DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED; } bIsUnique = (V_BOOL(&val)==VARIANT_TRUE); } } } } hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (!pIndexID) { indexName.Append(L"i_"); indexName.Append(tableName); indexName.Append(L"_"); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { indexName.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i+1 != cIndexColumnDescs) indexName.Append(L"_"); } } else indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //인덱스 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(ITableDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) return DB_E_DUPLICATEINDEXID; rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (bIsUnique) strQuery.Append(L"CREATE UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"CREATE INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); strQuery.Append(L" ("); for (DBORDINAL i = 0; i < cIndexColumnDescs; i++) { //컬럼 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), CW2A(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOCOLUMN; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); strQuery.Append(rgIndexColumnDescs[i].pColumnID->uName.pwszName); if (i + 1 != cIndexColumnDescs) strQuery.Append(L","); } strQuery.Append(L")"); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg); } if(ppIndexID) { DBID tmp; tmp.eKind = DBKIND_NAME; tmp.uName.pwszName = indexName; *ppIndexID = (DBID *)CoTaskMemAlloc(sizeof(DBID)); CopyDBIDs(*ppIndexID, &tmp); } AutoCommit(0); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDSession::DropIndex( /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pTableID, /* [unique][in] */ DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; CComBSTR tableName, indexName; CComBSTR strQuery; int hConn, hReq, rc; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pTableID) return E_INVALIDARG; ClearError(); hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) { return E_FAIL; } //테이블 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if(hReq<0) { ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n"); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOTABLE; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); cci_close_req_handle(hReq); tableName = pTableID->uName.pwszName; if (pIndexID) { bool indexFound = false; bool bIsUniqueIndex = false; indexName = pIndexID->uName.pwszName; //Index 이름 존재 여부 검사 hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CONSTRAINT, CW2A(pTableID->uName.pwszName), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return DB_E_NOINDEX; else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); while (1) { char* index_name; int isUnique; int ind; rc = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if (rc == CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 1, CCI_A_TYPE_INT, &isUnique, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); rc = cci_get_data(hReq, 2, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &index_name, &ind); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition)); if (!_wcsicmp(CA2W(index_name), indexName)) { indexFound = true; if (isUnique == 0) bIsUniqueIndex = true; break; } rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); if (!indexFound) return DB_E_NOINDEX; if (bIsUniqueIndex) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(indexName); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_ASYNC, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } else { CAtlArray<CStringA> rgIndexNames; CAtlArray<int> rgIndexTypes; hr = Util::GetIndexNamesInTable(hConn, CW2A(tableName), rgIndexNames, rgIndexTypes); if (FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; size_t cIndex = rgIndexNames.GetCount(); for(size_t i=0;i<cIndex;i++) { if (rgIndexTypes.GetAt(i) == 0) strQuery.Append(L"DROP UNIQUE INDEX "); else strQuery.Append(L"DROP INDEX "); strQuery.Append(rgIndexNames[i].GetBuffer()); strQuery.Append(L" ON "); strQuery.Append(tableName); if (i+1 != cIndex) strQuery.Append(L";"); } hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error); if (hReq < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error); if (rc < 0) { ATLTRACE2(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "%s\n", error.err_msg); return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IIndexDefinition), error.err_msg); } } AutoCommit(0); return hr; }
925  hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_CLASS, CW2A(table_name),
926  NULL, CCI_CLASS_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error);
927  if(hReq<0)
928  {
929  ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n");
930  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
931  }
932  rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error);
933  if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA)
934  return DB_E_NOTABLE;
935  else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
936  cci_close_req_handle(hReq);
937 
938  hReq = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(table_name),
939  CW2A(pColumnID->uName.pwszName), 0, &error);
940  if(hReq<0)
941  {
942  ATLTRACE2("cci_schema_info fail\n");
943  return E_FAIL;
944  }
945  rc = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error);
946  if(rc==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA)
947  return DB_E_NOCOLUMN;
948  else if (rc<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
949  cci_close_req_handle(hReq);
950 
951  strQuery.Append(L"ALTER ");
952  strQuery.Append(pTableID->uName.pwszName);
953  strQuery.Append(L" DROP ");
954  strQuery.Append(pColumnID->uName.pwszName);
955 
956  hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(strQuery), 0, &error);
957  if (hReq < 0)
958  {
959  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
960  }
961 
962  rc = cci_execute(hReq, CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL, 0, &error);
963  if (rc < 0)
964  {
965  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(ITableDefinition), error.err_msg);
966  }
967 
968  AutoCommit(0);
969 
970  return hr;
971 }
